class="textLockUp__content"><h2 class="textLockUp__title u-wordbreak type-heading-2"><span>FAQs</span></h2></div></div><div class="accordion-wrapper"><details class="accordion__item"><summary class="accordion__title type-subhead-4"><h3>What does Browserbase do?</h3><span class="accordion__icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="material-symbols-outlined" fill="currentColor" focusable="false" height="24" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M480-346.85 253.85-573 291-610.15l189 189 189-189L706.15-573 480-346.85Z"></path></svg></span></summary><div class="accordion__text" role="region" tabindex="0"><div class="accordion__body text stack type-body-4"><p>Browserbase is the complete platform for building and deploying browser agents that browse and interact with the web like humans. One API key gives your agents everything they need: headless browsers, agent identity, search, fetch, and deployment.</p></div></div></details><details class="accordion__item"><summary class="accordion__title type-subhead-4"><h3>What kinds of use cases do companies use Browserbase for?</h3><span class="accordion__icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="material-symbols-outlined" fill="currentColor" focusable="false" height="24" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M480-346.85 253.85-573 291-610.15l189 189 189-189L706.15-573 480-346.85Z"></path></svg></span></summary><div class="accordion__text" role="region" tabindex="0"><div class="accordion__body text stack type-body-4"><p>Teams use Browserbase to build browser agents for deep prospect research, competitive intelligence, lead enrichment, account monitoring, and any workflow that requires real interaction with live websites rather than static data.</p></div></div></details><details class="accordion__item"><summary class="accordion__title type-subhead-4"><h3>What is the difference between a browser agent and a search or fetch API?</h3><span class="accordion__icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="material-symbols-outlined" fill="currentColor" focusable="false" height="24" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M480-346.85 253.85-573 291-610.15l189 189 189-189L706.15-573 480-346.85Z"></path></svg></span></summary><div class="accordion__text" role="region" tabindex="0"><div class="accordion__body text stack type-body-4"><p>Search and fetch APIs see roughly 15% of the web. Browser agents can access the other 85%, including pages that require authentication, dynamic content, and complex interactions. If your agent needs to do more than read a cached page, it needs a browser.</p></div></div></details><details class="accordion__item"><summary class="accordion__title type-subhead-4"><h3>What frameworks does Browserbase support?</h3><span class="accordion__icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="material-symbols-outlined" fill="currentColor" focusable="false" height="24" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M480-346.85 253.85-573 291-610.15l189 189 189-189L706.15-573 480-346.85Z"></path></svg></span></summary><div class="accordion__text" role="region" tabindex="0"><div class="accordion__body text stack type-body-4"><p>Browserbase works with all major agent frameworks, including LangChain, CrewAI, and Mastra. Stagehand, our AI SDK for browser agents, gives developers Playwright-level control with AI-native primitives built in.</p></div></div></details><details class="accordion__item"><summary class="accordion__title type-subhead-4"><h3>Can I bring my own proxies?</h3><span class="accordion__icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="material-symbols-outlined" fill="currentColor" focusable="false" height="24" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M480-346.85 253.85-573 291-610.15l189 189 189-189L706.15-573 480-346.85Z"></path></svg></span></summary><div class="accordion__text" role="region" tabindex="0"><div class="accordion__body text stack type-body-4"><p>Yes.</p></div></div></details><details class="accordion__item"><summary class="accordion__title type-subhead-4"><h3>Can I run browsers on-prem?</h3><span class="accordion__icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="material-symbols-outlined" fill="currentColor" focusable="false" height="24" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M480-346.85 253.85-573 291-610.15l189 189 189-189L706.15-573 480-346.85Z"></path></svg></span></summary><div class="accordion__text" role="region" tabindex="0"><div class="accordion__body text stack type-body-4"><p>Yes. Reach out to discuss deployment options for your infrastructure.</p></div></div></details><details class="accordion__item"><summary class="accordion__title type-subhead-4"><h3>What regions are you in?</h3><span class="accordion__icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="material-symbols-outlined" fill="currentColor" focusable="false" height="24" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M480-346.85 253.85-573 291-610.15l189 189 189-189L706.15-573 480-346.85Z"></path></svg></span></summary><div class="accordion__text" role="region" tabindex="0"><div class="accordion__body text stack type-body-4"><p>Browserbase runs globally distributed infrastructure. Contact us for specific region availability.</p></div></div></details><details class="accordion__item"><summary class="accordion__title type-subhead-4"><h3>How is Browserbase related to Stagehand?</h3><span class="accordion__icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="material-symbols-outlined" fill="currentColor" focusable="false" height="24" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M480-346.85 253.85-573 291-610.15l189 189 189-189L706.15-573 480-346.85Z"></path></svg></span></summary><div class="accordion__text" role="region" tabindex="0"><div class="accordion__body text stack type-body-4"><p>Stagehand is the AI SDK for browser agents, built and maintained by Browserbase. It replaces rigid selectors with natural language interactions that self-heal when pages change. Together they form the core of the browser agent development experience.</p></div></div></details></div></div></fk-scroll-reveal></section></div><script>$RS("S:f","P:f")</script><script>$RC("B:2","S:2")</script><div hidden id="S:21"><li
